  387. I love that I can get this many colors for like $20. That's awesome. That bumps it up a star just for that reason alone.<br /><br />These are the things you will need to be prepared to do with these polishes:<br /><br />- Prepare yourself for the possibility of duplicate colors. My set came with all the colors promised, but so many other reviewers have said they got duplicates that I just sort of assumed when I ordered this that I would get dupes. So I was pleasantly surprised!<br /><br />- Use nail polish thinner. The formula is thicker than it really should be with nail art, so I have started putting about half a dropper of Seche Restore in the bottle and then rolling it before I even bother starting to put any of these lacquers on my nails. On the plus side, once I've done that, they spread beautifully and I like how vivid the colors are!<br /><br />- Close and roll/shake often. Even if you haven't put any nail polish thinner into this stuff, it seems to separate quickly. I can work with about three nails before I have to cap it and roll it again, or it gets too tacky to work with. Annoying for lacquer meant for nail art.<br /><br />- Trim the brushes. With every single bottle I've opened so far (I haven't used all the colors, but I've used at least half by now), the brush has had a bristle or two that sticks way, way out on the end. Some people might prefer this for detail work, and some people might have their own nail art brushes to work with. But if you don't, and if you plan on using the brushes that came in this bottle, I recommend taking your nail clippers or another pair of small scissors and just trimming the ends to make them angle the way that you're comfortable working with.<br /><br />- If you're using one of the colors to coat your whole nail, I recommend using two coats of base coat. Some of the colors are very heavily pigmented and the pigment is grainy. It's difficult to remove even with acetone. Using two coats of base coat before I put these colors on has helped with this issue.<br /><br />So - I paid cheap money, and got lots of somewhat cheap polish for my cheap money. I would say I still got better than I paid for, since I paid less than a dollar a bottle. Four stars, and I'll probably buy it again if I ever need to.
